Industry\tBackground\n\nAll\telectronic\tsignals\tfall\tinto\tone\tof\ttwo\tcategories,\tanalog\tor\tdigital.\tAnalog\tsignals,\talso\tknown\tas\tlinear\tsignals,\trepresent\treal-world\tphenomena,\tsuch\tas\ttemperature,\tpressure,\tsound,\tspeed and\tmotion.\tThis\tinformation\tcan\tbe\tdetected\tand\tmeasured\tusing\tanalog\tsensors\tby\tgenerating\tcontinuously-varying\tvoltages\tand\tcurrents.\tThe\tsignals\tfrom\tthese\tsensors\tare\tinitially\tprocessed\tusing analog\tmethods,\tsuch\tas\tamplification,\tfiltering\tand\tshaping.\tThey\tare\tthen\tusually\tconverted\tto\tdigital\tform\tfor\tstorage\tor\tfurther\tmanipulation.\tThe\tfurther\tmanipulation\tof\tthe\tsignals\tafter\tconversion to\tdigital\tform\tis\tcalled\t"digital\tsignal\tprocessing."\tDigital\tsignals\trepresent\tthe\t"ones"\tand\t"zeros"\tof\tbinary\tarithmetic\tand\tare\teither\ton\tor\toff.\tDigital\tsignals\tare\tfrequently\tconverted\tback\tto\tanalog form\tfor\tfunctions\tsuch\tas\tvideo\tdisplay,\taudio\toutput\tor\tcontrol.\tWe\trefer\tto\tthese\tmanipulations\tand\ttransformations\tas\t"real-world\tsignal\tprocessing."\n\nSignificant\tdevelopments\tin\tsemiconductor\ttechnology\tin\trecent\tyears\thave\tsubstantially\tincreased\tthe\tperformance\tand\tfunctionality\tof\tintegrated\tcircuits,\tor\tICs,\tused\tin\tsignal\tprocessing applications.\tThese\tdevelopments\tinclude:\n\n•\tthe\tability\tto\tcombine\tanalog\tand\tdigital\tsignal\tprocessing\tcapability\ton\ta\tsingle\tchip,\tthereby\tmaking\tpossible\tmore\thighly-integrated\tsolutions;\tand\n\n•\tthe\twidespread\tapplication\tof\tlow-cost,\thigh-performance\tmicroprocessor-based\tsystems,\twhich\tallows\tcustomers\tto\tconvert\tanalog\tinformation\tinto\tdigital\tinformation\tthat\tcan\tbe\tmanaged by\tthese\tmicroprocessors.\n\n# Digital\tSignal\tProcessing\tProducts\n\nDigital\tSignal\tProcessors\t(DSPs)\tcomplete\tour\tproduct\tportfolio.\tDSPs\tare\toptimized\tfor\thigh-speed\tnumeric\tcalculations,\twhich\tare\tessential\tfor\tinstantaneous,\tor\treal-time,\tprocessing\tof\tdigital Backlog\n\nBacklog\tat\tthe\tend\tof\tfiscal\t2009\twas\tapproximately\t$411\tmillion,\tup\tfrom\tapproximately\t$333\tmillion\tat\tthe\tend\tof\tfiscal\t2008.\tWe\tdefine\tbacklog\tas\tof\ta\tparticular\tdate\tto\tmean\tfirm\torders from\ta\tcustomer\tor\tdistributor\twith\ta\trequested\tdelivery\tdate\twithin\tthirteen\tweeks.\tBacklog\tis\timpacted\tby\tthe\ttendency\tof\tcustomers\tto\trely\ton\tshorter\n\nlead\ttimes\tavailable\tfrom\tsuppliers,\tincluding\tus,\tin\tperiods\tof\tdepressed\tdemand.\tIn\tperiods\tof\tincreased\tdemand,\tthere\tis\ta\ttendency\ttowards\tlonger\tlead\ttimes\tthat\thas\tthe\teffect\tof\tincreasing\tbacklog and,\tin\tsome\tinstances,\twe\tmay\tnot\thave\tmanufacturing\tcapacity\tsufficient\tto\tfulfill\tall\torders.\tAs\tis\tcustomary\tin\tthe\tsemiconductor\tindustry,\twe\tallow\tmost\torders\tto\tbe\tcancelled\tor\tdeliveries\tto\tbe delayed\tby\tcustomers\twithout\tsignificant\tpenalty.\tAccordingly,\twe\tbelieve\tthat\tour\tbacklog\tat\tany\ttime\tshould\tnot\tbe\tused\tas\tan\tindication\tof\tour\tfuture\trevenue.\n\nWe\ttypically\tdo\tnot\thave\tlong-term\tsales\tcontracts\twith\tour\tcustomers.\tIn\tsome\tof\tour\tmarkets\twhere\tend-user\tdemand\tmay\tbe\tparticularly\tvolatile\tand\tdifficult\tto\tpredict,\tsome\tcustomers\tplace orders\tthat\trequire\tus\tto\tmanufacture\tproduct\tand\thave\tit\tavailable\tfor\tshipment,\teven\tthough\tthe\tcustomer\tis\tunwilling\tto\tmake\ta\tbinding\tcommitment\tto\tpurchase\tall,\tor\teven\tany,\tof\tthe\tproduct.\tIn\tother Recoverability\tof\tthese\tassets\tis\tmeasured\tby\tcomparison\tof\ttheir\tcarrying\tvalue\tto\tfuture\tundiscounted\tcash\tflows\tthat\tthe\tassets\tare\texpected\tto\tgenerate\tover\ttheir\tremaining\teconomic\tlives.\tIf\tsuch assets\tare\tconsidered\tto\tbe\timpaired,\tthe\timpairment\tto\tbe\trecognized\tin\tearnings\tequals\tthe\tamount\tby\twhich\tthe\tcarrying\tvalue\tof\tthe\tassets\texceeds\ttheir\tfair\tvalue\tdetermined\tby\teither\ta\tquoted\tmarket price,\tif\tany,\tor\ta\tvalue\tdetermined\tby\tutilizing\ta\tdiscounted\tcash\tflow\ttechnique.\tAlthough\twe\thave\trecognized\tno\tmaterial\timpairment\tadjustments\trelated\tto\tour\tproperty,\tplant,\tand\tequipment\tand identified\tintangible\tassets\tduring\tthe\tpast\tthree\tfiscal\tyears,\texcept\tthose\tmade\tin\tconjunction\twith\trestructuring\tactions,\tdeterioration\tin\tour\tbusiness\tin\tthe\tfuture\tcould\tlead\tto\tsuch\timpairment adjustments\tin\tfuture\tperiods.\tEvaluation\tof\timpairment\tof\tlong-lived\tassets\trequires\testimates\tof\tfuture\toperating\tresults\tthat\tare\tused\tin\tthe\tpreparation\tof\tthe\texpected\tfuture\tundiscounted\tcash\tflows. in\timpairment\tcharges,\twhich\tcould\thave\ta\tmaterial\tadverse\timpact\ton\tour\tresults\tof\toperations.\tIn\taddition,\tin\tcertain\tinstances,\tassets\tmay\tnot\tbe\timpaired\tbut\ttheir\testimated\tuseful\tlives\tmay\thave turn,\tmay\tresult\tin\tan\tincrease\tor\tdecrease\tto\tour\ttax\tprovision\tin\ta\tsubsequent\tperiod.\n\nOn\tNovember\t4,\t2007\t(the\tfirst\tday\tof\tour\t2008\tfiscal\tyear),\twe\tadopted\tnew\taccounting\tprinciples\ton\taccounting\tfor\tuncertain\ttax\tpositions.\tThese\tprinciples\trequires\tcompanies\tto\tdetermine\tthat factors\twould\tresult\tin\tthe\trecognition\tof\ta\ttax\tbenefit\tor\tan\tadditional\tcharge\tto\tthe\ttax\tprovision.\n\nIn\tthe\tordinary\tcourse\tof\tglobal\tbusiness,\tthere\tare\tmany\ttransactions\tand\tcalculations\twhere\tthe\tultimate\ttax\toutcome\tis\tuncertain.\tSome\tof\tthese\tuncertainties\tarise\tas\ta\tconsequence\tof\tcost
